\\n343: def _variant(versions: version.WebEngineVersions) -> Variant:\\n344:     \\\"\\\"\\\"Get the dark mode variant based on the underlying Qt version.\\\"\\\"\\\"\\n345:     env_var = BUG: The code uses the wrong option name ('threshold.foreground' instead of\n   'threshold.text') when trying to replace the setting.\n\n4. RESULT: The copy_replace_setting method can't find a setting with option name\n   'threshold.foreground' and either:\n   - Raises a ValueError (if strict), or\n   - Returns the original definition without the replacement\n\n5. CONSEQUENCE: The Qt 6.4 definition still has chromium_key='TextBrightnessThreshold'\n   instead of the correct 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold'. Since Chromium no longer\n   recognizes 'TextBrightnessThreshold', the setting is silently ignored by the browser.\n\nThis test demonstrates that the replacement failed and the wrong setting name is used.\n\"\"\"\n\nimport sys\nsys.path.insert(0, '/app')\n\nfrom qutebrowser.browser.webengine import darkmode\n\n\ndef test_qt64_has_correct_text_threshold_setting():\n    \"\"\"\n    Test that Qt 6.4 definition has a 'threshold.text' setting.\n\n    This test verifies that the threshold.text setting exists in the Qt 6.4\n    definition. If the definition was created without this setting, the test\n    should fail.\n    \"\"\"\n    variant_64 = darkmode.Variant.qt_64\n    definition_64 = darkmode._DEFINITIONS[variant_64]\n\n    # Find the threshold.text setting in the qt_64 definition\n    threshold_text_setting = None\n    for setting in definition_64._settings:\n        if setting.option == 'threshold.text':\n            threshold_text_setting = setting\n            break\n\n    assert threshold_text_setting is not None, (\n        \"Qt 6.4 definition is missing the 'threshold.text' setting. \"\n        \"The copy_replace_setting method may have failed to find the setting.\"\n    )\n\n\ndef test_qt64_has_renamed_text_threshold_chromium_key():\n    \"\"\"\n    Test that Qt 6.4 uses 'ForegroundBrightnessThreshold' for text threshold.\n\n    This is the critical test that demonstrates the bug.
